```
CHLDID07  "2007 INTERVIEW NUMBER"                NUM(5.0)
2007 PSID Main Family Identifier

The values for this variable represent the 2007 interview number of the family in which
this individual was included in 2007.

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

Interview number

```

```
Value/Range

   1 - 8,332

```

```
Count

 1,506

```

```
%

100.00
```

```
CHLDSN07  "CYPSN 2007"                     NUM(2.0)
2007 PSID Sequence Number

This sequence number variable provides a means of identifying an individual's status with
regard to the family unit at the time of the PSID main family 2007 interview.

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

Sequence number of individuals in the PSID family at the
time of the 2007 main family interview

```
```
Value/Range

     1 - 20
```

```
Q33K20   "TIME GO TO BED WEEKNIGHTS 07"            NUM(5.0)
K20. What time do you usually go to bed on weeknights? Please type the time you usually
go to bed in this format: Type in hour first, then minutes. The colon will automatically
appear to separate the hour and minutes. Use A for "AM" and P for "PM". For example, if
you go to bed at 9 o'clock in the evening, then enter "900P". Please remember that
midnight is "1200A" and noon is "1200P."
See the note at Q33K1.

This variable was collected as hours and minutes (e.g., 9:00 PM). Those values were
translated into number of seconds past midnight (12:00 AM). If midnight (12:00AM) was
reported, it was assigned 60 seconds so that if recoded to hours and minutes, it will
become 0:01.

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

NA; DK; refused
```

```
     99,999
```

```
CDI_07   "CDI SHORT FORM 07"                  NUM(2.0)
Child Depression Inventory 02

This variable is the raw score of the CDI. Items L16a, c, d, f, i were recoded to: 1=0,
2=1, 3=2; and items L16b, e, g, h, j were recoded to: 1=2, 2=1, 3=0. The 10 items were
then summed if valid data points were available on all 10 items.

See the note at Q33L1.
```
